<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄργανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órganon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рган</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">órgan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́ргана</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рганы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рганов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> organ</li>
<li>body, agency, authority
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рганы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>órgany</b> vlásti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">government bodies</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:законодательный.html>законода́тельный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рган</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakonodátelʹnyj <b>órgan</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">legislative body</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рган</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ispolnítelʹnyj <b>órgan</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">executive body</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>ме́стный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рган</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méstnyj <b>órgan</b> vlásti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">local government</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рганы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:здравоохранение.html>здравоохране́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>órgany</b> zdravooxranénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">health authorities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руководящий.html>руководя́щие</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рганы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rukovodjáščije <b>órgany</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">governing <b>authorities</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>organ, publication
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ежедневный.html>ежедне́вные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орган.html>о́рганы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ježednévnyje <b>órgany</b> pečáti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the daily organs of the press</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***организация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a> (942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">organizácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>organization, arrangement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>organizácija</b> proizvódstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">organization of production</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>organization
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объединённый.html>Объединённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нация.html>на́ций</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Organizácija Obʺjedinjónnyx Nácij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">United Nations Organization</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>setup, structure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сети</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>organizácija</b> seti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">networking</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***организм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зм</a> (1378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">organisme</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">organízm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́змы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́змов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>system of organs making up the body of a living thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">перееда́ть <a href = vnd.unilang:вредный.html>вре́дно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зма</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Perejedátʹ vrédno dlja náševo <b>organízma</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Overeating is bad for our <b>bodies</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>organism (living thing, usually a small and simplistic one)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a complex structure or mechanism</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:организоваться.html>организова́ться</a> (23980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организовать.html>организова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">organizovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организоваться.html>организова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">organizovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">организо́вываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be/become organized</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:организовать.html>организова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">organizovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This verb can also be used in the present and future tenses as in imperfective.
</p>

***органический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:органический.html>органи́ческий</a> (9185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">organ(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:органический.html>органи́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">organíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>organic</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдер</a> (11193)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">órder</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>ордера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>ордеро́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">document</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">órder</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдеры</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>ордера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>о́рдеров</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ордер.html>ордеро́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***ординарный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ординарный.html>ордина́рный</a> (24934)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ōrdinārius</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ординарный.html>ордина́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ordinárnyj</span>)

***орех.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a> (4636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orěxъ</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">arrë</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walnut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄρυα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">árua</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walnut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">riẽksts</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">òrah</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oréx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nut <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tree; seed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американский.html>америка́нский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">amerikánskij <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Brazil nut (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Bertholletia_excelsa" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Bertholletia excelsa"><i>Bertholletia excelsa</i></a></span>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">American <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бразильский.html>брази́льский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">brazílʹskij <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Brazil nut (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Bertholletia_excelsa" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Bertholletia excelsa"><i>Bertholletia excelsa</i></a></span>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Brazilian <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесной.html>лесно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lesnój <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hazelnut; butternut (<i>Juglans cinerea</i>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">forest <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">séryj <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">butternut (<i>Juglans cinerea</i>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">gray <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čórnyj <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">black walnut (<i>Juglans nigra</i>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">black <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грецкий.html>гре́цкий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gréckij <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">walnut</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Greek <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китайский.html>кита́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kitájskij <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">peanut</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Chinese <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земляной.html>земляно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zemljanój <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">peanut</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">earth <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">муска́тный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">muskátnyj <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">nutmeg</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">musky <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кедровый.html>кедро́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kedróvyj <b>oréx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pine nut</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">cedar <b>nut</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>walnut wood</li>
<li>nut coal; chestnut coal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cocaine</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oréx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ореховый.html>оре́ховый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oréxovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ореховый.html>оре́ховая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорлупа.html>скорлупа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oréxovaja</b> skorlupá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nut</b>shell</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> walnut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ореховый.html>оре́ховый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлеб.html>хлеб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oréxovyj</b> xleb</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>walnut</b> bread</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>walnut, nut-brown <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:орешник.html>оре́шник</a> (16731)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oréx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешник.html>оре́шник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oréšnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешник.html>оре́шника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешник.html>оре́шники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орешник.html>оре́шников</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оре́шниковый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hazel</li>
<li>hazel grove</li>
<li>commercial grade of anthracite</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">originál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинал.html>оригина́лов</a></b>)
</p>

***оригинальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оригинальный.html>оригина́льный</a> (4873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оригинальный.html>оригина́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">originálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
